After giving effect to the First Amendment, the Incremental Term Loans shall bear interest at a rate per annum equal to a forward-looking term rate that is based on SOFR for a tenor of three&#160;(3) months<span style="background:#ffffff;"> (with a credit spread adjustment of 0.15%&#160;per annum)</span> (or another applicable reference rate, as determined pursuant to the terms of the Amended Credit Agreement), plus an applicable margin of 7.75%. Except as otherwise provided in the First Amendment and the Amended Credit Agreement, the terms applicable to the Incremental Term Loans, including the maturity applicable thereto, are the same as those applicable to the initial term loan facility funded on the Original Closing Date. Other than the foregoing, all other material provisions of the Credit Agreement remain materially unchanged.&#160;</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Each of the <a name="_9kMH2J6ZWu59978IeRnndLuEM"></a>Loan Parties as debtor, grantor, pledgor, guarantor, assignor, or in other any other similar capacity in which such <a name="_9kMH3K6ZWu59978IeRnndLuEM"></a>Loan Party grants liens or security interests in its property or otherwise acts as accommodation party or guarantor, as the case may be, hereby (a)&#160;ratifies and reaffirms all of its payment and performance obligations, contingent or otherwise, under each of the Loan Documents to which it is a party (after giving effect hereto) and (b)&#160;to the extent such <a name="_9kMH4L6ZWu59978IeRnndLuEM"></a>Loan Party granted liens on or security interests in any of its property pursuant to any such Loan Document as security for or otherwise guaranteed the Borrower&#8217;s and the other <a name="_9kR3WTr26645EaOkkaIrB3p0pWn4K5sdW084xBK"></a>Loan Parties&#8217; &#8220;Secured Obligations&#8221; or any term of like nature (in each case as defined in the applicable Loan Document) under or with respect to the Loan Documents, ratifies and reaffirms such guarantee and grant of security interests and liens and confirms and agrees that such security interests and liens hereafter secure all of <a name="_9kR3WTr266467ZLct9uhSLpxtm095BG"></a>such obligations as amended hereby. Each of the <a name="_9kMH5M6ZWu59978IeRnndLuEM"></a>Loan Parties hereby consents to this First Amendment and acknowledges that each of the Loan Documents remains in full force and effect and is hereby ratified and reaffirmed. The execution of this First Amendment shall not (a)&#160;operate as a waiver or release of any right, power, claim, lien, security interest, entitlement or remedy of the Administrative Agent or the Lenders, (b)&#160;constitute a waiver of any provision of any of the Loan Documents or serve to effect a novation of the <a name="_9kMHG5YVt488689bNevBwjUNrzvo2B7DI"></a>Secured Obligations, or (c)&#160;operate as a release of any Loan Party from any covenant, warranty or obligation created by or contained herein or in any of the Loan Documents.</div><div style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:12pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-top:12pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:36pt;"><font style="display:inline-block;font-family:'(normal text)';min-width:36pt;text-decoration-line:none;text-indent:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:nowrap;">13.</font><u style="text-decoration-color:#000000;text-decoration-line:underline;text-decoration-style:solid;">Integration; </u><u style="text-decoration-color:#000000;text-decoration-line:underline;text-decoration-style:solid;">Entire</u><u style="text-decoration-color:#000000;text-decoration-line:underline;text-decoration-style:solid;"> Agreement</u>.
